YOU MAID ME LOUGH
Brownie recipe Classic Fudgy Brownies Yields: 16-20 brownies Prep time: 15 minutes Bake time: 25-30 minutes Ingredients:  * 1 cup (2 sticks) unsalted butter, melted  * 2 cups granulated sugar  * 4 large eggs  * 1 teaspoon vanilla extract  * 1 cup all-purpose flour  * Â¾ cup unsweetened cocoa powder (Dutch-processed for a darker, less bitter brownie is great, but natural works too)  * Â½ teaspoon baking powder  * Â¼ teaspoon salt  * 1 cup chocolate chips or chunks (optional, but highly recommended for extra fudginess!) Equipment:  * 9x13 inch baking pan  * Parchment paper (optional, but makes removal much easier)  * Large mixing bowl  * Whisk  * Spatula Instructions:  * Preheat Oven & Prepare Pan: Preheat your oven to 350Â°F (175Â°C). Lightly grease a 9x13 inch baking pan. For easier removal, line the pan with parchment paper, leaving an overhang on the two longer sides (this creates "handles").  * Melt Butter & Combine with Sugar: In a large mixing bowl, combine the melted butter and granulated sugar. Whisk until well combined and smooth.  * Add Eggs & Vanilla: Add the eggs one at a time, whisking well after each addition. Stir in the vanilla extract. The mixture should be smooth and glossy.  * Combine Dry Ingredients: In a separate medium bowl, whisk together the flour, cocoa powder, baking powder, and salt.  * Combine Wet and Dry: Gradually add the dry ingredients to the wet ingredients, mixing with a spatula until just combined. Be careful not to overmix; overmixing can lead to tougher brownies.  * Stir in Chocolate Chips (Optional): If using, gently fold in the chocolate chips or chunks.  * Pour into Pan & Bake: Pour the brownie batter evenly into the prepared baking pan.  * Bake: Bake for 25-30 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out with moist crumbs, but not wet batter. Be careful not to overbake, as this will result in dry brownies.  * Cool: Let the brownies cool completely in the pan on a wire rack before cutting. This is crucial for fudgy brownies that hold their shape. If you cut them while warm, they'll be delicious but a bit messy.  * Cut and Serve: Once completely cooled, use the parchment paper handles to lift the brownies out of the pan. Cut into squares and enjoy! Tips for Success:  * Don't Overbake! This is the golden rule for fudgy brownies. When in doubt, err on the side of slightly underbaked.  * Cool Completely: Patience is key! Cooling allows the brownies to set up properly, giving you that perfect fudgy texture.  * Room Temperature Eggs: While not strictly necessary, room temperature eggs incorporate more smoothly into the batter.  * Dutch-Processed Cocoa: If you want a truly dark and rich chocolate flavor, opt for Dutch-processed cocoa powder.  * Variations: Feel free to add nuts (walnuts or pecans are great), a swirl of peanut butter, or even a sprinkle of sea salt on top before baking. Enjoy
